        <div class="description__text description__text--rich">
         <section class="show-more-less-html" data-max-lines="5">
          <div class="show-more-less-html__markup show-more-less-html__markup--clamp-after-5 relative overflow-hidden">
           <p>
            <strong>
             This position is within the
             <em>
              Optima Medical Center
             </em>
             team,
            </strong>
            <strong>
             a growing company with a collaborative culture.
            </strong>
           </p>
           <p>
            <br/>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             <em>
              Joinrs AI
             </em>
             's summary of the opportunity:
            </strong>
            Join
            <strong>
             Optima Medical Center
            </strong>
            as a remote
            <strong>
             Data Analyst
            </strong>
            with a
            <strong>
             bachelor’s degree
            </strong>
            and
            <strong>
             experience in data analysis tools.
            </strong>
            You will collect, analyze, and report data to support business decisions and collaborate with teams.
            <strong>
             They offer a competitive salary, flexible remote work, professional growth, and inclusive culture.
            </strong>
           </p>
           <p>
            <br/>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             Job Location
            </strong>
            : Chicago.
           </p>
           <p>
            <br/>
           </p>
           <p>
            <em>
             The selection process will be entirely managed by Optima Medical Center.
            </em>
           </p>
           <p>
            <br/>
           </p>
           <p>
            --
           </p>
           <p>
            <br/>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             Job Description:
            </strong>
           </p>
           <p>
            We are seeking a detail-oriented and analytical Remote Data Analyst to join our growing team. In this role, you will be responsible for collecting, processing, and analyzing data to support various business initiatives. You will work closely with different departments to identify trends, generate insights, and help drive data-informed decision-making.
           </p>
           <p>
            <br/>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             Key Responsibilities:
            </strong>
           </p>
           <p>
            - Collect, clean, and validate data from various sources to ensure accuracy and reliability.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Analyze complex datasets to identify trends, patterns, and insights that can support business strategies.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Create and maintain reports and dashboards that communicate insights effectively to stakeholders.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Collaborate with cross-functional teams to understand their data needs and provide analytical support.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Perform ad-hoc analysis and present findings in a clear and concise manner.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Assist in developing predictive models and algorithms to enhance decision-making processes.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Stay updated on industry trends and best practices in data analysis and visualization.
           </p>
           <p>
            <br/>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             Qualifications:
            </strong>
           </p>
           <p>
            - Bachelor’s degree in Data Science, Statistics, Mathematics, Computer Science, or a related field.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Proven experience as a Data Analyst or similar role.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Proficiency in data analysis tools (e.g., Excel, SQL, Python, R).
           </p>
           <p>
            - Experience with data visualization tools (e.g., Tableau, Power BI, or similar).
           </p>
           <p>
            - Strong analytical and problem-solving skills.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Excellent communication skills, with the ability to present complex information in an understandable format.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Ability to work independently and manage multiple projects simultaneously in a remote environment.
           </p>
           <p>
            <br/>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             Preferred Qualifications:
            </strong>
           </p>
           <p>
            - Experience with machine learning techniques and statistical modeling.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Knowledge of database management and data warehousing concepts.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Familiarity with cloud computing platforms and big data technologies.
           </p>
           <p>
            <br/>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             What We Offer:
            </strong>
           </p>
           <p>
            - Competitive salary and benefits package.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Flexible work environment with remote work options.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Opportunities for professional growth and development.
           </p>
           <p>
            - Collaborative and inclusive company culture.
           </p>
          </div>
